==Usage==
<pre>{{Armor_Data|<variable1>|<variable2>|...}}</pre>


==Variables==

***<stat_name>
***allstats

***<ability_type>

==Global==
All attributes that are shared between all other attributes in the same layer are moved to a global layer

For example, if all |movementmultiplier's under Abilities|Primary| are the same, they will be moved to Abilities|Primary|global

See Example 2 for more information


==All==
All sub-layers can also call |all for a list of all unique attributes
For example, 

<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|all}}</pre>

will output a list of all items

For example, 

<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|<itemname>|all}}</pre>

will output a list of all attributes of a particular

See example 1 and 6 for more information


==Examples==
Note, some variables may not be applicable to all item categories.
The below examples are for the Arming Sword, which only exists in Weapon_Data.
Other item categories, like Misc_Data, may have different variables, and obviously don't have others, like abilities

===Example 1===
All stats of the Arming Sword
<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|stats|all}}</pre>
Outputs {{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|stats|all}}



===Example 2===
All shared attributes for Primary attacks of Arming Sword
<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|abilities|Primary|global}}</pre>
Outputs {{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|abilities|Primary|global}}



===Example 3===
Damagefalloff widget of Longbow
<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|Longbow|damagefalloff}}</pre>
Outputs {{Armor_Data|Longbow|damagefalloff}}



===Example 4===
All non-artifact rarities of the Arming Sword
<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|rarities}}</pre>
Outputs {{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|rarities}}



===Example 5===
Invslots size image of Arming Sword
<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|invslots}}</pre>
Outputs {{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|invslots}}



===Example 6===
All attributes of primary abilities of Arming Sword
<pre style="width:fit-content;">{{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|abilities|Primary|all}}</pre>
Outputs {{Armor_Data|Arming Sword|abilities|Primary|all}}



</noinclude>
